src=\"https://media.nomadicmatt.com/2020/thgupdate4.jpg\" width=\"675\" height=\"395\" alt=\"A luxurious and spacious first class seat on an airplane \"><br />\n<strong>Posted</strong>: 7/13/2020 | July 13th, 2020</p>\n<p>Hey everybody,</p>\n<p>Just a quick update today to let you know we just updated our amazing travel hacking guide! </p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/travel-blogs/travel-hacking-1-million-miles-per-year/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Travel hacking</a> is the art of collecting frequent-flier points and miles to get free flights, hotels, tours, and more. It allows you to have those once-in-a-lifetime experiences: an over-water bungalow in <a href=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/travel-guides/french-polynesia-travel-tips/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">Tahiti</a>, a first-class flight with a shower, an <a href=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/travel-blogs/six-of-the-greatest-safaris-in-africa/\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\">African safari</a>, a visit to the Galápagos Islands, or that dream trip to the French Riviera.</p>\n<p>Travel hacking is the single best way to save money on travel. </p>\n<p>I’ve been travel hacking for over a decade — and it is the linchpin of all my money-saving advice. It helps me save tens of thousands of dollars on flights, accommodation, and transportation every year.</p>\n<p>I don’t need to spend extra money, take special trips to earn more points, or get into debt. I do this with my normal, everyday spending.</p>\n<p>Sure, we can’t travel right now but, when we can, having some points and miles for free travel will really help keep costs down! </p>\n<p>In this update, we:</p>\n<ol>\n<li>Updated the rules on credit cards</li>\n<li>Updated information for all our credit cards and resources</li>\n<li>Added new tricks on how to redeem points and miles</li>\n<li>Updated the section on using gift cards to generate free miles</li>\n<li>Added more ways to manufacture spending to generate free miles (including ones not normally shared publicly)</li>\n<li>Updated information on airline and hotel loyalty programs and their requirements</li>\n<li>Updated everything else that needed to be updated! </li>\n</ol>\n<p>This book is the best resource for those looking to get into travel hacking — or those who have started but are sick and tired of trying to figure it all out on their own. </p>\n<p>You don’t need to search hundreds of blogs or spend hours figuring this out. My book lays it all out in a step-by-step format, so you just have to follow the guide and you’ll be raking in hundreds of thousands of miles without ever needing to travel.</p>\n<p><a href=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/cart/?add-to-cart=147424\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" target=\"_blank\"><img src=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat.jpg\" alt=\"A cover to Nomadic Matt's travel hacking guide\" width=\"225\" height=\"292\" class=\"alignright size-full wp-image-207687\" srcset=\"https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat.jpg 679w, https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat-231x300.jpg 231w, https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat-300x390.jpg 300w, https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat-600x779.jpg 600w, https://www.nomadicmatt.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/07/NM_Travel_Hacking_flat-400x520.jpg 400w\" sizes=\"(max-width: 225px) 100vw, 225px\" /></a>This book covers: </p>\n<ul>\n<li>The history and philosophy behind travel hacking</li>\n<li>How to use credit scores to your advantage</li>\n<li>How to spot and get the best-earning reward cards</li>\n<li>How to master the ins and outs of loyalty programs</li>\n<li>How to maximize your everyday spending for bonus points</li>\n<li>The secret art of earning points for FREE</li>\n<li>How to always find an award flight or hotel room</li>\n<li>Where to discover the best travel deals</li>\n<li>The tools and resources travelers use to unlock secret fares and deals</li>\n<li>BONUS: The guide also includes step-by-step cheat sheets so you can keep these tips handy</li>\n</ul>\n<p>I know we can’t travel right now, but when we can, wouldn’t it be nice to have tens of thousands of points at your disposal so you can do so for free?
